length theſe ſhips wyll goe well head ſeaof ship ſayle wel bowlyne harde pulled alſo ſayle well hed sea ſay ship ſtande cloſe winde ſuch place grating tyde doth cauſe ſea come agaynſt head bowes ship thoſe ſhips haue reaſonable length well breſted bowed buttockes ſterne ſhip bigge full quartered behinde bee reaſonable lancke sterne thoſe ſhippes goe ſayle well hed sea ſo wyll beare good ſayleof wyll let hynder way goyng shippe alſo thoſe shippes wyll ryde yll rode ancor sea broadneſſe buttockes shippe dooth ſo thruſte downe head shippe sea eſpecially bowes ship narrow ſlender sea ſhall flye
